  "content": "import pandas as pd\nimport os\n\n\ndef process_json_and_append_to_csv(json_data, csv_file, principal):\n    \"\"\"\n    Process the JSON data and append it to the CSV file\n    Args: json_data (string): JSON data to process\n    Args: csv_file (string): CSV file to append to\n    returns: None\n    \"\"\"\n\n    # Load JSON data into a Python dictionary\n    # data = json.loads(json_data)\n\n    # Create an empty DataFrame with the required columns\n    df = pd.DataFrame(\n        columns=[\n            \"Principal\",\n            \"Allowed Action\",\n            \"Denied Action\",\n            \"Resource\",\n            \"Conditions\",\n        ]\n    )\n\n    # Create a list to store DataFrame rows\n    rows = []\n\n    # Populate the DataFrame with the JSON data\n    for action in json_data:\n        for allowed_resource in json_data[action][\"Allow_resources\"]:\n            rows.append(\n                {\n                    \"Principal\": principal,\n                    \"Allowed Action\": action,\n                    \"Denied Action\": \"\",\n                    \"Resource\": allowed_resource,\n                    \"Conditions\": json_data[action][\"Allow_conditions\"],\n                }\n            )\n\n        for denied_resource in json_data[action][\"Deny_resources\"]:\n            rows.append(\n                {\n                    \"Principal\": principal,\n                    \"Allowed Action\": \"\",\n                    \"Denied Action\": action,\n                    \"Resource\": denied_resource,\n                    \"Conditions\": json_data[action][\"Deny_conditions\"],\n                }\n            )\n\n    # Concatenate the rows to the DataFrame\n    df = pd.concat([df, pd.DataFrame(rows)], ignore_index=True)\n\n    # Check if the CSV file exists, and write the header if necessary\n    if not os.path.isfile(csv_file):\n        df.to_csv(csv_file, index=False, mode=\"w\", header=True)\n    else:\n        df.to_csv(csv_file, index=False, mode=\"a\", header=False)\n",

  "content": "import boto3\nfrom botocore.config import Config\nimport os\nimport json\nfrom concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor\n\nfrom IAMActionHunter.lib.statement_parser import enumerate_actions_resources_for_statements\n\n\ndef get_all_iam_policies(target_aws_profile):\n    \"\"\"\n    Get all IAM policies for roles and users for the specified AWS profile\n    Args: target_aws_profile (str): AWS profile to use for authentication\n    Returns: None\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def ensure_list(item):\n        \"\"\"\n        Ensure that the item is a list\n        Args: item (object): item to check\n        returns: list: item as a list\n        \"\"\"\n        if isinstance(item, list):\n            return item\n        else:\n            return [item]\n\n    def get_role_policies(role):\n        role_name = role[\"RoleName\"]\n        statements = []\n\n        # Get statetments for inline policies attached to the role\n        response = iam.list_role_policies(RoleName=role_name)\n        for policy_name in response[\"PolicyNames\"]:\n            statement = iam.get_role_policy(RoleName=role_name, PolicyName=policy_name)[\"PolicyDocument\"][\"Statement\"]\n            statements += ensure_list(statement)\n\n        # Get statements for managed policies attached to the role\n        response = iam.list_attached_role_policies(RoleName=role_name)\n        for policy in response[\"AttachedPolicies\"]:\n            policy_arn = policy[\"PolicyArn\"]\n            policy_name = policy_arn.split(\":\")[-1]\n            version_id = iam.get_policy(PolicyArn=policy_arn)[\"Policy\"][\"DefaultVersionId\"]\n            statement = iam.get_policy_version(PolicyArn=policy_arn, VersionId=version_id)[\"PolicyVersion\"][\"Document\"][\n                \"Statement\"\n            ]\n            statements += ensure_list(statement)\n\n        role_output = enumerate_actions_resources_for_statements(statements)\n\n        # Save policies to file\n        output_file = os.path.join(roles_output_dir, f\"{role_name}.json\")\n        with open(output_file, \"w\") as f:\n            json.dump(role_output, f)\n\n    def get_user_policies(user):\n        user_name = user[\"UserName\"]\n        statements = []\n\n        # Get stetaments for inline policies attached to the user\n        response = iam.list_user_policies(UserName=user_name)\n        for policy_name in response[\"PolicyNames\"]:\n            statement = iam.get_user_policy(UserName=user_name, PolicyName=policy_name)[\"PolicyDocument\"][\"Statement\"]\n            statements += ensure_list(statement)\n\n        # Get  statements for managed policies attached to the user\n        response = iam.list_attached_user_policies(UserName=user_name)\n        for policy in response[\"AttachedPolicies\"]:\n            policy_arn = policy[\"PolicyArn\"]\n            policy_name = policy_arn.split(\":\")[-1]\n            version_id = iam.get_policy(PolicyArn=policy_arn)[\"Policy\"][\"DefaultVersionId\"]\n            statement = iam.get_policy_version(PolicyArn=policy_arn, VersionId=version_id)[\"PolicyVersion\"][\"Document\"][\n                \"Statement\"\n            ]\n            statements += ensure_list(statement)\n\n        # Get statements for managed policies attached to the user's groups\n        response = iam.list_groups_for_user(UserName=user_name)\n        for group in response[\"Groups\"]:\n            group_name = group[\"GroupName\"]\n            response = iam.list_attached_group_policies(GroupName=group_name)\n            for policy in response[\"AttachedPolicies\"]:\n                policy_arn = policy[\"PolicyArn\"]\n                policy_name = policy_arn.split(\":\")[-1]\n                version_id = iam.get_policy(PolicyArn=policy_arn)[\"Policy\"][\"DefaultVersionId\"]\n                statement = iam.get_policy_version(PolicyArn=policy_arn, VersionId=version_id)[\"PolicyVersion\"][\n                    \"Document\"\n                ][\"Statement\"]\n                statements += ensure_list(statement)\n        user_output = enumerate_actions_resources_for_statements(statements)\n\n        # Create IAM client\n    config = Config(retries=dict(max_attempts=10))\n    iam = session.client(\"iam\", config=config)\n\n    # Get AWS account number\n    sts = session.client(\"sts\")\n    account_id = sts.get_caller_identity().get(\"Account\")\n\n    print(f\"Downloading IAM policies for account {account_id}...\")\n\n    # Paginate through all users\n    users = []\n    marker = None\n    while True:\n        if marker:\n            response = iam.list_users(Marker=marker)\n        else:\n            response = iam.list_users()\n        users.extend(response[\"Users\"])\n        if response[\"IsTruncated\"]:\n            marker = response[\"Marker\"]\n        else:\n            break\n\n    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=10) as executor:\n        # Save policies for all roles\n        for role in roles:\n            executor.submit(get_role_policies, role)\n\n        # Save policies for all users\n        for user in users:\n            executor.submit(get_user_policies, user)\n\n    print(f\"Finished downloading IAM policies for account {account_id}.\")\n    print(f\"Processing files for {account_id}...\")\n",

  "content": "from policyuniverse.statement import Statement\n\n\nclass ExtendedStatement(Statement):\n    \"\"\"\n    Extends the Statement class to add the notresources and conditions properties\n    \"\"\"\n\n    @property\n    def notresources(self):\n        # If the statement has NotResource, add a notresources attribute to the PU statement object\n        if \"NotResource\" in self.statement:\n            if isinstance(self.statement.get(\"NotResource\"), str):\n                return set([self.statement.get(\"NotResource\")])\n            return set(self.statement.get(\"NotResource\"))\n        else:\n            return set()\n\n    @property\n    def conditions(self):\n        # Add a conditions attribute to the PU statement object\n        return self.statement.get(\"Condition\") or {}\n\n\ndef convert_sets_to_lists(obj):\n    \"\"\"\n    Converts sets to lists in a dictionary\n    Args: obj (dict): a dictionary object\n    returns: dict: a dictionary object with sets converted to lists\n    \"\"\"\n    if isinstance(obj, set):\n        return list(obj)\n    elif isinstance(obj, dict):\n        return {key: convert_sets_to_lists(value) for key, value in obj.items()}\n    elif isinstance(obj, list):\n        return [convert_sets_to_lists(element) for element in obj]\n    else:\n        return obj\n\n\ndef enumerate_actions_resources_for_statements(list_of_statements):\n    \"\"\"\n    Enumerates resources and expanded actions for a list of statements\n    Args: list_of_statements (list): list of statement JSON objects from a policy\n    returns: dict: a dictionary of actions with the following structure:\n\n    {\n        \"someAction\": {\n            \"Deny_resources\": [],\n            \"Deny_conditions\": [],\n            \"Allow_resources\": [],\n            \"Allow_conditions\": []\n        },\n        \"someOtherAction\": {\n            \"Deny_resources\": [],\n            \"Deny_conditions\": [],\n            \"Allow_resources\": [],\n            \"Allow_conditions\": []\n        }\n    }\n    \"\"\"\n    results = {}\n\n    def new_action_dict():\n        # returns a new action dictionary\n        return {\n            \"Deny_resources\": set(),\n            \"Deny_conditions\": [],\n            \"Allow_resources\": set(),\n            \"Allow_conditions\": [],\n        }\n\n    for st in list_of_statements:\n        try:\n            statement = ExtendedStatement(st)\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(e)\n            print(\"[!] Error parsing statement\")\n            continue\n\n        # iterate through the found query actions\n        for action in statement.actions_expanded:\n            effect_key = statement.effect\n\n            # Set the action dictionary to the results dictionary if it exists\n            # otherwise create a new action dictionary\n            action_dict = results.get(action, new_action_dict())\n\n            # Add resources to the Deny_resources set if there is a notresources and effect is Allow\n            if statement.notresources and statement.effect == \"Allow\":\n                updated_resources = action_dict[\"Deny_resources\"].union(statement.notresources)\n                action_dict.update({\"Deny_resources\": updated_resources})\n\n            if statement.notresources and statement.effect == \"Deny\":\n                # Add a condition in this case since it means access is denied\n                # but does not mean any other access is allowed\n                # TODO maybe a better way to do this but for now here we are.\n                action_dict[\"Allow_conditions\"].append({\"StringEquals\": {\"aws:ResourceArn\": statement.notresources}})\n\n            # Update the Allow or Deny resources\n            updated_resources = action_dict[f\"{effect_key}_resources\"].union(statement.resources)\n            action_dict.update({f\"{effect_key}_resources\": updated_resources})\n\n            # Add conditions if any exist\n            if statement.conditions:\n                action_dict[f\"{effect_key}_conditions\"].append(statement.conditions)\n\n            # Update the results for the actions\n            results[action] = action_dict\n\n    return convert_sets_to_lists(results)\n",

def process_cli_args():
    """
    Parse the command-line arguments
    returns: argparse object: command-line arguments
    """
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        description=(
            "Collect all policies for all users/roles in an AWS account and then query the policies for permissions."
        )
    )
    group = parser.add_mutually_exclusive_group(required=True)
    parser.add_argument(
        "--profile",
        help="The name of the AWS profile to use for authentication for user/role collection.",
    )
    group.add_argument(
        "--account",
        help="Account number to query.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--query", help="Permissions to query. A string like: s3:GetObject or s3:* or s3:GetObject,s3:PutObject"
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--role",
        help="Filter role to query.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--user",
        help="Filter user to query.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--all-or-none",
        help="Check if all queried actions are allowed, not just some.",
        action="store_true",
        default=False,
    )
    group.add_argument(
        "--collect",
        help="Collect user and role policies for the account.",
        action="store_true",
        default=False,
    )
    group.add_argument(
        "--list",
        help="List accounts available to query.",
        action="store_true",
        default=False,

10. WRITE /app/IAMActionHunter/lib/create_csv.py
import pandas as pd
import os


def process_json_and_append_to_csv(json_data, csv_file, principal):
    """
    Process the JSON data and append it to the CSV file
    Args: json_data (string): JSON data to process
    Args: csv_file (string): CSV file to append to
    returns: None
    """

    # Load JSON data into a Python dictionary
    # data = json.loads(json_data)

    # Create an empty DataFrame with the required columns
    df = pd.DataFrame(
        columns=[
            "Principal",
            "Allowed Action",
            "Denied Action",
            "Resource",
            "Conditions",
        ]
    )

    # Create a list to store DataFrame rows
    rows = []

    # Populate the DataFrame with the JSON data
    for action in json_data:
        for allowed_resource in json_data[action]["Allow_resources"]:
            rows.append(
                {
                    "Principal": principal,
                    "Allowed Action": action,
                    "Denied Action": "",
                    "Resource": allowed_resource,
                    "Conditions": json_data[action]["Allow_conditions"],
                }
            )

        for denied_resource in json_data[action]["Deny_resources"]:
            rows.append(
                {
                    "Principal": principal,
                    "Allowed Action": "",
                    "Denied Action": action,
                    "Resource": denied_resource,
                    "Conditions": json_data[action]["Deny_conditions"],
                }
            )

    # Concatenate the rows to the DataFrame
    df = pd.concat([df, pd.DataFrame(rows)], ignore_index=True)

    # Check if the CSV file exists, and write the header if necessary
    if not os.path.isfile(csv_file):
        df.to_csv(csv_file,
... (truncated)

def get_all_iam_policies(target_aws_profile):
    """
    Get all IAM policies for roles and users for the specified AWS profile
    Args: target_aws_profile (str): AWS profile to use for authentication
    Returns: None

        """
        Ensure that the item is a list
        Args: item (object): item to check
        returns: list: item as a list
        """
        if isinstance(item, list):
            return item
        else:
            return [item]

            statements += ensure_list(statement)

            statement = iam.get_policy_version(PolicyArn=policy_arn, VersionId=version_id)["PolicyVersion"]["Document"][
                "Statement"
            ]

12. WRITE /app/IAMActionHunter/lib/statement_parser.py
from policyuniverse.statement import Statement


class ExtendedStatement(Statement):
    """
    Extends the Statement class to add the notresources and conditions properties
    """

    @property
    def notresources(self):
        # If the statement has NotResource, add a notresources attribute to the PU statement object
        if "NotResource" in self.statement:
            if isinstance(self.statement.get("NotResource"), str):
                return set([self.statement.get("NotResource")])
            return set(self.statement.get("NotResource"))
        else:
            return set()

    @property
    def conditions(self):
        # Add a conditions attribute to the PU statement object
        return self.statement.get("Condition") or {}


def convert_sets_to_lists(obj):
    """
    Converts sets to lists in a dictionary
    Args: obj (dict): a dictionary object
    returns: dict: a dictionary object with sets converted to lists
    """
    if isinstance(obj, set):
        return list(obj)
    elif isinstance(obj, dict):
        return {key: convert_sets_to_lists(value) for key, value in obj.items()}
    elif isinstance(obj, list):
        return [convert_sets_to_lists(element) for element in obj]
    else:
        return obj

    {
        "someAction": {
            "Deny_resources": [],
            "Deny_conditions": [],
            "Allow_resources": [],
            "Allow_conditions": []
        },
        "someOtherAction": {
            "Deny_resources": []

13. WRITE /app/IAMActionHunter/lib/text_formatter.py
from colorama import Fore, Style


class color:
    """
    Colorama color class
    Usage: print(color.red("This is red text"))
    Args: string (str): String to color
    """

    def red(string):
        return f"{Fore.RED}{string}{Style.RESET_ALL}"

    def green(string):
        return f"{Fore.GREEN}{string}{Style.RESET_ALL}"

    def yellow(string):
        return f"{Fore.YELLOW}{string}{Style.RESET_ALL}"

import toml
try:
    with open('/app/pyproject.toml', 'r') as f:
        config = toml.load(f)
    print("✓ pyproject.toml is valid TOML")
    
    # Print the dependencies found
    deps = config.get('tool', {}).get('poetry', {}).get('dependencies', {})
    print(f"\nProduction dependencies ({len(deps)-1}):")  # -1 for python version
    for dep in sorted(deps.keys()):
        if dep != 'python':
            print(f"  - {dep}: {deps[dep]}")
    
    dev_deps = config.get('tool', {}).get('poetry', {}).get('group', {}).get('dev', {}).get('dependencies', {})
    print(f"\nDevelopment dependencies ({len(dev_deps)}):")
    for dep in sorted(dev_deps.keys()):
        print(f"  - {dep}: {dev_deps[dep]}")
    
except Exception as e:
    print(f"✗ Error: {e}")

15. $ cat << 'EOF' > /tmp/verify_deps.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3

# Parse the pyproject.toml file manually
with open('/app/pyproject.toml', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Extract production dependencies
import re

# Find [tool.poetry.dependencies] section
deps_start = content.find('[tool.poetry.dependencies]')
deps_end = content.find('[tool.poetry.group.dev]')
deps_section = content[deps_start:deps_end]

# Extract all dependency lines
dep_lines = [line.strip() for line in deps_section.split('\n') if '=' in line and not line.startswith('[')]

print("=== PRODUCTION DEPENDENCIES ===")
for line in dep_lines:
    print(f"  {line}")

# Find [tool.poetry.group.dev.dependencies] section
dev_deps_start = content.find('[tool.poetry.group.dev.dependencies]')
dev_deps_end = content.find('[build-system]')
dev_deps_section = content[dev_deps_start:dev_deps_end]

dev_dep_lines = [line.strip() for line in dev_deps_section.split('\n') if '=' in line and not line.startswith('[')]

print("\n=== DEV DEPENDENCIES ===")
for line in sorted(dev_dep_lines):
    print(f"  {line}")

print("\n=== SUMMARY ===")
print(f"Production dependencies: {len(dep_lines)}")
print(f"Development dependencies: {len(dev_dep_lines)}")
EOF

16. $ cat << 'EOF' > /tmp/verify_completeness.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Verify all requirements are in pyproject.toml"""

import re

# Read the requirements files
with open('/app/requirements.txt', 'r') as f:
    req_lines = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip() and not line.startswith('#')]

with open('/app/dev-requirements.txt', 'r') as f:
    dev_lines = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip() and not line.startswith('#')]

# Extract package names from requirements
def extract_package_name(req_line):
    """Extract package name from requirement line"""
    match = re.match(r'([a-zA-Z0-9_\-]+)', req_line)
    return match.group(1) if match else None

req_packages = set(extract_package_name(line) for line in req_lines if line)
dev_packages = set(extract_package_name(line) for line in dev_lines if line)

print("=== PRODUCTION REQUIREMENTS ===")
print(f"Found {len(req_packages)} packages:")
for pkg in sorted(req_packages):
    print(f"  ✓ {pkg}")

print("\n=== DEVELOPMENT-ONLY REQUIREMENTS ===")
dev_only = dev_packages - req_packages
print(f"Found {len(dev_only)} development-only packages:")
for pkg in sorted(dev_only):
    print(f"  ✓ {pkg}")

# Read pyproject.toml
with open('/app/pyproject.toml', 'r') as f:
    pyproject_content = f.read()

# Extract dependencies from pyproject
def extract_deps_from_section(section_text):
    """Extract dependency package names"""
    packages = set()
    for line in section_text.split('\n'):
        if '=' in line and not line.startswith('['):
            match = re.match(r'([a-zA-Z0-9_\-]+)\s*=', line)
            if match:
                packages.add(match.group(1))
    return packages

# Find production deps
prod_start = pyproject_content.find('[tool.poetry.dependencies]')
prod_end = pyproject_content.find('[tool.poetry.group.dev]')
prod_section = pyproject_content[prod_start:prod_end]
pyproject_prod_deps = extract_deps_from_section(prod_section)

# Find dev deps
dev_start = pyproject_content.find('[tool.poetry.group.dev.dependencies]')
dev_end = pyproject_content.find('[build-system]')
dev_section = pyproject_content[dev_start:dev_end]
pyproject_dev_deps = extract_deps_from_section(dev_section)

print("\n=== VERIFICATION ===")
# Check if all production requirements are in pyproject
missing_prod = req_packages - pyproject_prod_deps
if missing_prod:
    print(f"✗ Missing production dependencies: {missing_prod}")
else:
    print(f"✓ All {len(req_packages)} production dependencies are in pyproject.toml")

# Check if all dev-only requirements are in pyproject
missing_dev = dev_only - pyproject_dev_deps
if missing_dev:
    print(f"✗ Missing dev dependencies: {missing_dev}")
else:
    print(f"✓ All {len(dev_only)} development-only dependencies are in pyproject.toml")

print("\n=== FINAL STATUS ===")
if not missing_prod and not missing_dev:
    print("✅ COMPLETE: All dependencies from requirements files are now in pyproject.toml")
else:
    print("❌ INCOMPLETE: Some dependencies are missing")
EOF
